namespace = red_turban
country_event = { 
	id = red_turban.1
	title = "red_turban.1.t"
	desc = "red_turban.1.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	trigger = { 
		culture_group = chinese_group
		AND = { 
			OR = { 
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
				is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
				is_subject_of_type = muscovite_tributary_state
			}
		}
		AND = { 
			NOT = { 
				num_of_cities = 20
			}
			any_neighbor_country = { 
				culture_group = chinese_group
				ai = yes
				num_of_cities = 100
				legitimacy = 70
				AND = { 
					num_of_cities = 1
					NOT = { 
						tag = AAA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 10
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.ISTHATSO"
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					num_of_cities = 20
				}
				any_neighbor_country = { 
					culture_group = chinese_group
					num_of_cities = 100
					legitimacy = 70
					AND = { 
						num_of_cities = 1
						NOT = { 
							tag = AAA
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_neighbor_country = { 
				limit = { 
					culture_group = chinese_group
					num_of_cities = 100
					legitimacy = 70
					AND = { 
						num_of_cities = 1
						NOT = { 
							tag = AAA
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { 
					id = red_turban.2
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

				limit = {

						}
